# readme-generator
A smart web tool that instantly reads your zipped project folder, extracts its file structure, detects technologies used (React, Node, HTML, etc.), and generates a clean, professional README.md file â€” all within seconds.

## ğŸ“– Overview

A React-based web application scaffolded with Vite or Create React App. Styled using Tailwind CSS.

## ğŸš€ Getting Started

1. Clone the repository:
```bash
git clone https://github.com/Nikhilsharma00101/readme-generator.git
```

2. Install dependencies:
```bash
npm install
```

3. Run the app:
```bash
npm run dev
```

## ğŸ§° Technologies Used

- Node.js
- React
- Tailwind CSS
